This file describes the coauthorship network of 1559 scientists.
First the names are listed with numerical ids.  
Then the edges are given as triples: the first two items are the ids; the third is the number of papers
they coauthored which can be interpreted as an edge weight and can be initially disregarding in defining
the network.  Also some edges join a vertex to itself and these can also be ignored.
From https://open.umich.edu/sites/default/files/1446/CoAuthorshipNetwork.net
